s website. If the party does not have online access, they may call the dedicated phone number for the department as referenced in the local telephone directory between the hours of 2:00 p.m. and 4:00 p.m. on the court day before 
the hearing and receive the tentative ruling. If you do not call the court and the opposing party by 4:00 p.m. the court day before the hearing, no hearing will be held.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5198427

\par }\pard \ltrpar\ql \li0\ri0\sl453\slmult0\widctlpar\wrapdefault\aspalpha\aspnum\faauto\adjustright\rin0\lin0\itap0\pararsid7480003 {\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 A. Grounds for Relief.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 
\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
 On application, the court may, on any terms as may be just, relieve a party or his or her legal representative from a judgment, dismissal, order, or other proceeding taken against him or her through his or her mistake, inadvertence,

\par 
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 B. Policy of Law Favors Trial on Merits.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
 The policy of the law is that controversies should be heard and disposed of on their merits (}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \i\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 Fasuyi v. Permatex, Inc.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
 (2008) 167 Cal. App. 4th 681, 694\endash 703, 84 Cal. Rptr. 3d 351; }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \i\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 Berman v. Klassman}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
 (1971) 17 Cal. App. 3d 900, 909, 95 Cal. Rptr. 417).
\par 
\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 C. Court Has Wide Discretion in Granting Relief.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979  A trial court has wide di}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824 
scretion to grant relief under }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 Code of Civil Procedure Section 473 (}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \i\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 Berman v. Klassman}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 
\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979  (1971) 17 Cal. App. 3d 900, 909, 95 Cal. Rptr. 417).

\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 D. Liberal Construction of Statute}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid15408138\charrsid5593979 .}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid15408138\charrsid5593979  }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 
\ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 Code of}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824  Civil Procedure Section 473(b)}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
 is a remedial measure to be liberally construed, and any doubts existing as to the propriety of setting aside a default thereunder will be resolved in favor of a hearing on the merits (}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \i\insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979 
Berman v. Klassman}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid5593979  (1971) 17 Cal. App. 3d 900, 910, 95 Cal. Rptr. 417).}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824

\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid7480003 R}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid3619234 . Judgment Roll When Complaint Not Answered.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid11011902 
 If the complaint is not answered by any defendant, the following papers, without being attached together, constitute th
e judgment roll: the summons, with the affidavit or proof of service; the complaint; the request for entry of default with a memorandum endorsed thereon that the default of the defendant in not answering was entered, and a copy of the judgment; if defenda
nt has appeared by demurrer, and the demurrer has been overruled, then notice of the overruling thereof served on defendant\rquote 
s attorney, together with proof of the service; and in case the service is made by publication, the affidavit for publication of summons, and the order directi}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3493753 ng the publication of summons (}{\rtlch\fcs1 
\af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \insrsid3932824\charrsid11011902 Code Civ. Proc. \'a7 670(a)).

\par }{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid7480003 T}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0 \b\insrsid3932824\charrsid4813514 . Compliance With Statutory Provisions Governing Service of Process Is Required.}{\rtlch\fcs1 \af0 \ltrch\fcs0
